```cpp
            while(x >= cur)
                res += x / cur, cur *= 5ll;
            return res;
        };
        ll l1 = 0, r1 = K * 5ll;
        while(l1 < r1){
            ll mid = (l1 + r1) >> 1;
            if(calc(mid) < K)
                l1 = mid + 1;
            else r1 = mid;
        }
        ll l2 = 0, r2 = (K + 1) * 5ll;
        while(l2 < r2){
            ll mid = (l2 + r2) >> 1;
            if(calc(mid) <= K)
                l2 = mid + 1;
            else r2 = mid;
        }
        return r2 - r1;
    }
};
```

# 798
用一个数组

```cpp
class Solution {
public:
    int bestRotation(vector<int>& A) {
        int n = A.size(), tot = 0;
        vector<int> cnt(n + 1, 0);
        for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i) 
            if (i >= A[i])
                ++cnt[i - A[i]], ++tot;
        int p = 0, maxi = -1;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i){
            if (tot > maxi) maxi = tot, p = i;
            tot -= cnt[i];
            if (i - A[i] >= 0) 
                --cnt[i - A[i]];
            else ++cnt[n + i - A[i]];
            if (A[i] < n) ++tot;
        }
        return p;
    }
};
```

# 805

## 方法一
DP
```cpp
class Solution {
public:
    bool splitArraySameAverage(vector<int>& A) {
        int n = A.size(), sum = 0;
        if(n <= 1) return false;
        for (int i: A)
            sum += i;
        vector<vector<bool> > f((n >> 1) + 1, vector<bool>(1 + (n >> 1) * sum / n, 0));
        f[0][0] = true;
        for (int i = 0; i < n; ++i){
            for (int j = (n >> 1); j >= 1; --j)
                for (int k = (n >> 1) * sum / n; k >= A[i]; --k){
                    if(f[j - 1][k - A[i]])
                        f[j][k] = true;
                }
        }
        for (int i = (n >> 1); i >= 1; --i){
            if(i * sum % n) continue;
            int targ = i * sum / n;
            if(f[i][targ]) return true;
        }
        return false;
    }
};
```
